lgo ma Mari ner is t he sec o n d a n d fi nal vessel i n a

wit h t he first vessel i n t he series, Algo bay , delivere d i n 
2 0 1 0.  T he  vessel  was  delivere d  fr o m  C he n g  Xi  
S hi p b uil di ng Heavy I n d ustries C o., Lt d i n May.
W hile b ot h Algo ma Mari ner a n d Algobay  are sister s hi ps 
wit h res pect t o carg o carryi ng a n d disc harge ca pa bilities a n d 
have i de ntical vessel f ore b o dies, Algo ma Mari ner  has a very 
differe nt aft secti o n, mac hi nery a n d acc o m m o dati o n areas. 
T he ster n h ull f or m of t he Algo ma Mari ner  is a c o m pletely 
ne w desig n f or t he vessel by Delta mari n, desig ners of 
Alg o ma’s ne w E q ui n ox Class dry- b ul k carg o vessels. T he 
o pti mise d h ull a n d r u d der have bee n desig ne d t o i m prove 
f uel efficie ncy a n d re d uce wa ke.
T his ne w vessel is p o were d by a si ngle sl o w s pee d e ngi ne 
w hic h pr ovi des better f uel efficie ncy. T his c o m bi ne d wit h 
t he c o ntr olla ble pitc h pr o peller a n d a m o der n a dva nce d 
c o ntrol syste m t hat i nter prets t he p o wer de ma n d fro m t he 
bri dge a n d res p o n ds wit h t he m ost efficie nt c o m bi nati o n of 
e ngi ne s pee d a n d pro peller pitc h at a ny give n l oa d, givi ng a 
sig nifica nt i m prove me nt i n perf or ma nce c o m pare d t o ot her 
vessels c urre ntly i n t he b ul k carrier fleet. 
T he electric p o wer ge nerati o n a n d distri b uti o n syste m als o 
ta kes f ull a dva ntage of electr o nic c o ntr ol a n d m o nit ori ng 
fro m t he sa me platf or m as t he pro p ulsi o n c o ntrol syste m.  A 
p o wer ma nage me nt syste m ( P M S) m o nit ors vessel p o wer

o ngo River was delivere d t o Belgi u m- base d D E M E at 
t he begi n ni ng of 2 0 1 1 fr o m I H C Dre dgers B. V. T he 
vessel  is  t he  latest  i n  mega  traili ng  s ucti o n  h o p per  
dre dgers f or D E M E.
T he c o ntract bet wee n D E M E N. V. a n d I H C Dre dgers 
f or t he desig n, c o nstr ucti o n, a n d delivery of t he s hi p was 
sig ne d i n Dece m ber 2 0 0 8 wit h t he keel layi ng ta ki ng 
place o n 1 5 Dece m ber 2 0 0 9 a n d c o m missi o ne d as of 
mi d- 2 0 1 1. 
T he vessel is fitte d wit h hig h-tec h e q ui p me nt o n b oar d, 
ma ki n g  it  o ne  of  t he  hi g hest  perf or mi n g  a n d  m ost 
ec o n o mical dre dgers o n t o day’s mar ket. T he na me Co ngo 
River  fits i nt o t he series of w orl d rivers w h ose na mes have 
bee n give n t o s o me of D E M E’s large dre dgers. Ot her 
exa m ples of vessel na mes t hat fit wit h t his t he mi ng are 
Pearl River, Nile River a n d A mazo ne . 
Co ngo River  is a n i n n ovative a n d versatile vessel, very 
ma n oe uvra ble d ue t o its large bea m ( 3 8 m) a n d s h ort 
le n gt h  ( 1 6 8 m)  a n d  de pl oya ble  f or  ma n y  differe nt  
p ur p oses. Beca use of its s hall o w dra ug ht, t he s hi p ca n 
o perate at a li mite d de pt h eve n w he n f ully l oa de d. Co ngo 
River ca n be efficie ntly de pl oye d i n p orts, c ha n nels, or f or

1 5 0 0 k W retracta ble t hr uster, t w o 1 9 0 0 k W t u n nel t hr usters 
a n d t w o azi m ut h t hr usters wit h a p o wer o ut p ut of 3 0 0 0 k W.

f orecastle, o pe n water ty pe ster n fra me, si ngle r u d der a n d

e ngi ne. T he vessel has a c o nti n u o us dec k fr o m ste m t o 
ster n, tra nsverse b ul k hea ds a n d d o u ble b ott o m i n way of 
t he  car g o  h ol d  part  a n d  i n  e n gi ne  r o o m;  wit h  t he  
pr o p ulsi o n mac hi nery a n d livi ng q uarters i ncl u di ng t he 
navigati o n bri dge t o be l ocate d aft of t he vessel.

e na bles her t o carr y t he Da nger o us Carg oes. T he vessel 
has bee n desig ne d t o carr y grai n, ir o n ore, c oal, h ot c oil 
a n d ca n l oa d t he t w o-layers of steel c oil weig hi ng u p t o 
2 0t o n nes, w hic h is i n disti ncti o n fr o m t he ol d series.

are pr otecte d by t he d o u ble h ull str uct ure i n t he t o p si de 
wi ng ta n ks, b ut t he diesel oil st orage ta n ks are of si ngle 
h ull  str uct ure  i n  e n gi ne  r o o m  d o u ble  b ott o m  i n  
c o m plia nce wit h M A R P O L A n nex. 1 C h. 3 Reg. 1 2 A 
P h. 1 1 “ Acci de ntal oil f uel o utfl o w perf or ma nce sta n dar d”

ta n ks c o ul d be use d f or l o w s ul p h ur H F O ta n k at t he 
B uyer’s discreti o n. T he carg o s pace is divi de d i nt o five

aers k Sara is a ver y lar ge cr u de carrier ( V L C C) 
t hat  was  deli vere d  fr o m  S T X  offs h ore  &  
S hi p b uil di n g  t o  A. P  M øller- Maers k  i n  May.  T he  
vessel’s  desi g n  was  i nte n de d  t o  re d uce  waste  e ner gy  
a n d e missi o ns a n d it has bee n fitte d wit h t he latest i n 
e ner gy savi n g feat ures.
T he vessel is desi g ne d as a n ocea n- g oi n g cr u de oil 
ta n ker  dri ve n  b y  a  si n gle  scre w  diesel  e n gi ne.  
Acc o m m o dati o n  i ncl u di n g  na vi gati o n  bri d ge  a n d  
e n gi ne r o o m are l ocate d aft of t he vessel, wit h t he car g o 
area c o nsisti n g of tri ple car g o oil ta n ks ( p ort, star b oar d 
a n d ce ntre) divi de d by b ul k hea ds ( p ort, star b oar d a n d 
ce ntre) a n d o ne pair of sl o p ta n ks ( p ort & star b oar d) 
wit h d o u ble b ott o m a n d d o u ble h ull. T he vessel has 1 5 
car g o ta n ks a n d t w o sl o p ta n ks wit h a t otal ca pacity of 
a p pr oxi mately 3 5 2, 8 3 4 m
3. T he aft b o dy wit h tra ns o m 
ster n is use d as a steeri n g gear c o m part me nt, fres h 
water ta n ks a n d aft pea k ta n k. F ore b o dy wit h b ul b o us 
b o w is use d f or f ore pea k ta n ks, c hai n l oc kers, v oi d 
s pace a n d b os u n st ore. 
T he vessel is desig ne d t o hei g hte n e ner gy efficie ncy by 
a p plyi n g a Wi de C h or d Ti p a n d Waste Heat Rec over y 
Syste m ( W H R S), w hic h s witc hes heat of e missi o n gas 
fr o m t he diesel e n gi ne t o electric p o wer. T he Wi de 
C h or d Ti p re d uces n oise a n d vi brati o n a n d i m pr oves 
t he pr o p ulsi o n efficie nc y. T he W H R S ca n re use n ot 
o nly waste heat fr o m t he e n gi ne b ut als o stea m fr o m 
t he  b oilers  w hic h  offers  a  7 %  decrease  i n  car b o n 
di oxi de, s o t he E ner gy Efficie ncy Desi g n I n dex ( E E DI) 
ca n  be  re d uce d  wit h  ar o u n d  5 %  f uel  sa vi n gs.  At  
1 5 k n ots,  t he  vessel  has  a  f uel  c o ns u m pti o n  of  
9 4t o n nes/ day i ncl u di n g t he re d ucti o n ac hieve d by t he 
W H R S. I n a d diti o n t he vessel has t he latest ge nerati o n 
of electr o nicall y c o ntr olle d diesel e n gi nes, e na bli n g 
m ore efficie nt f uel c o ns u m pti o n at var yi n g s pee ds 
( m ore t ha n 1 % f uel c o ns u m pti o n re d ucti o n).
A n i n n ovati ve life b oat dr o p-i n ball release s yste m 
devel o pe d by Na dir o wit h A. P M øller- Maers k is fitte d 
t o t he life b oats. T he syste m is desi g ne d as a n off-l oa d 
s yste m  wit h  a  h y dra ulic  o n-l oa d  f u ncti o nalit y  i n

ta n ks are utilise d as se gre gate d ballast ta n ks.

nat ural or c o nce ntrate d ora n ge j uice i n its 1 4  1 7. 5 m 
hi g h ta n ks ma de of stai nless steel. T w o bi g ger ta n ks

3.

2 0 0 0 m

t he tec h n ol o gy a p plie d i n t he f o o d i n d ustr y t o av oi d 
t h e  i m p erf e cti o ns  w hi c h  mi g ht  c a us e  t h e

u nit has its o w n access fr o m t he mai n dec k, as well as

la ne meters f or a ra nge of ve hicles over five dec ks.

T he € 1 1 0 milli o n i n vest me nt fr o m Ste na will gi ve t he 
ferr y o perat or a 3 0 % i ncrease i n frei g ht ca pacit y. After 
a s mall frei g ht rise is 2 0 1 0 Ste na belie ve d t hat ha vi n g 
lar ger vessels was t he wa y f or war d wit h de ma n d f or 
f urt her frei g ht ca pacit y risi n g. Ste n a Tr a ns p orter  is t he

f or frei g ht traffic.
Ste n a Tr a ns p orter  has t he ca pacit y of 4 0 5 0 la ne- meters 
( 2 6 0 frei g ht u nits) a n d 3 0 0 passe n gers o ver f o ur dec ks. 
T he f o ur fi xe d dec ks ( N o. 1, 3, 5, 7) are use d f or trailers, 
wit h  o ne ster n ra m p/ d o or e na bli n g e xter nal access t o

5) f or i nter nal traffic fl o w.  Da n ger o us car g oes are l oa de d 
o n dec k 5 a n d 7.

o n b oar d, w hic h c o nsist mai nl y of t w o bert h ca pacit y t hat 
are l ocate d o n dec k 8 a n d dec k 9. Dec k 7 pr o vi des t he mai n 
p u blic s paces wit h t w o differe nt t y pes of l o u n ges wit h a 
lar ge bar, 1 7 0 seati n g ca pacit y resta ura nt, i nter net area a n d 
ga mi n g area.  T he p u blic s paces a n d ca bi n areas were  
desi g ne d b y Da nis h arc hitect Stee n Friis Desi g n, wit h t he 
i nteri or o utfitti n g w or k f or passe n ger p u blic s paces carrie d 
o ut b y S we dis h Sca n mari ne Mari ne Gr o u p.
Ste n a Tr a ns p orter  has bee n b uilt t o meet t he hi g hest  
e n vir o n me ntal sta n dar ds of e ner g y & f uel efficie nc y a n d t o 
f ulfil Ll o y ds re gister’s E n vir o n me ntal Pr otecti o n n otati o n,

ca bi ns, t he vi brati o n le vel is bel o w t he l o wer li mit of I S O 
6 9 5 4- 2 0 0 0 a n d t he n oise le vel is 1 3 d B l o wer t ha n t he li mit

T he C P P pr o p ulsi o n s yste m utilises a fl oati n g fre q ue nc y

he 7 9 0 0 u nit large car a n d tr uc k carrier Tugela  was

rolli ng carg oes, i ncl u di ng cars, hig h & heavy rolli ng carg oes

ca n ge nerate a b o ut 1 1 0 0 k W of electric p o wer, c overi ng t he 
electrical o ut p ut of o ne set of ge nerat or e ngi nes, t here by 
re d uci ng C O2 e missi o ns as a res ult of re d uce d r u n ni ng 
ti me of ge nerat or e ngi nes w hic h b ur n m ore f uel d uri ng sea 
g oi ng. Tugela  is als o fitte d wit h a R olls- R oyce Pr o mas 
i ntegrate d  pr o peller  r u d der  syste m  w hic h  als o  offers  
i ncrease d  pr o p ulsive  efficie ncy  a n d  savi n g  3 3 %  of  
pr o p ulsi o n p o wer. 
Mai n a n d a uxiliary e ngi nes c o m ply wit h t he re d uce d 
N Ox e missi o n li mits sti p ulate d by I M O Tier II. T he maj or 
electricity c o ns u mers s uc h as t he mai n c o oli ng sea water 
p u m p, is fre q ue ncy c o ntrolle d by a n e nergy savi ng syste m. 
T he water ballast treat me nt syste m i nstalle d o n b oar d has 
bee n delivere d by Wil hel mse n Tec h nical Sol uti o n.

w hic h ca n acc o m m o date 7 9 0 0 cars, i ncl u di ng five lifta ble 
dec ks i ncl u di ng pr o digi o us heig ht cleara nce a n d i ncrease d 
u nif or m l oa d a n d axle l oa d t hat are hig hly be neficial t o heavy

ale  Brasil is  t he  first  4 0 0, 0 0 0 d wt  ore  carrier  t o  be

E ngi neeri ng C o., Lt d ( D S M E) i n A pril 2 0 1 1, w hic h will be

I n 2 0 0 8 Vale place d or ders f or 1 2 4 0 0, 0 0 0 d wt ‘ Vale max’ 
s hi ps t o be c o nstr ucte d by Jia ngs u R o ngs he ng Heavy  
I n d ustries i n C hi na a n d or dere d seve n m ore vessels fr o m 
So ut h Korea n D S M E i n 2 0 0 9. I n a d diti o n 1 6 m ore s hi ps of 
si milar size will be b uilt i n C hi na a n d So ut h Korea f or ot her 
s hi p pi ng c o m pa nies, a n d c hartere d t o Vale u n der l o ng-ter m 
c o ntracts. At t he e n d of 2 0 1 1 Vale a n n o u nce d t hat it has 
deci de d t o sell t he s hi ps it pla n ne d t o o w n itself t o ot her 
s hi p pi ng c o m pa nies a n d c harter t he m bac k.
T he e ngi neeri ng of Vale Brasil  was de ma n di ng d ue t o t he 
s pecific l oa di ng patter ns base d o n t he act ual tra de ro ute wit h 
o perati o n  c o n diti o ns  bei ng  ta ke n  i nt o  c o nsi derati o n  
acc or di ng t o t he differe nt ro utes a n d b u n keri ng.
Vale Brasil  is 3 6 2 m i n le ngt h overall, 6 5 m wi de a n d has a 
l oa di ng ca pacity of 4 0 0, 0 0 0 d wt. T he carg o s pace c o nsists of 
seve n carg o h ol ds, wit h six c orr ugate d tra nsverse b ul k hea ds 
bet wee n eac h of t he carg o h ol ds, eac h wit h u p per a n d l o wer 
st o ol. T he wi ng ta n ks are use d f or ballast water ta n ks, f uel 
ta n ks or voi d s paces.
Vale Brasil  has a n ass ure d l oa di ng efficie ncy wit h D N V’s 
efficie nt l oa di ng n otati o n E L- 2. T he de- ballast ca pacity of 
t he vessel at l oa di ng bert h pri or t o c o m me nce me nt of 
l oa di ng, i ncl u di ng arra nge me nt of ballast ta n ks a n d releva nt 
pi pi ng syste m, meets wit h t he re q uire me nts f or t he average 
l oa di ng rates.

a n d a b o ut half of t he t otal saili ng ti me of t he vessel will be i n 
ballast, t he h ull f or m has bee n o pti mise d n ot o nly f or t he 
desig n draft b ut als o at t he ballast c o n diti o n a n d a pre-s wirl 
stat or is i nstalle d at t he ster n fra me i n fro nt of t he pro peller 
as a n e nergy savi ng device.
